european_noble_mod_category = { 
	
    andrei_vladimirovich = { 
	
	    icon = decision_eng_abdication_crisis
		
		available = {
		    has_country_flag = royal_election
			has_government = monarchist
			monarchist > 0.4
			NOT = { has_global_flag = andrei_vladimirovich_flag }
		}
		
		fire_only_once = yes
		
		visible = { 
		    has_government = monarchist
            has_country_flag = never_had_monarchy			
			has_country_flag = royal_election
			NOT = { has_country_flag = president_king }
			NOT = { has_country_flag = had_monarchy }
			NOT = { has_country_flag = monarchy_in_place }
			NOT = { has_global_flag = andrei_vladimirovich_flag }
		}	
		
		complete_effect = {
		    clr_country_flag = royal_election
			set_country_flag = monarchist_nation
			set_global_flag = andrei_vladimirovich_flag
			kill_country_leader = yes
			create_country_leader = {
					name = "Andrei Alexandrovich Romanov"
					picture = "gfx/leaders/Monarchs/Andrei_Vladimirovich.tga"
					expire = "1981.1.1"
     				ideology = constitutional_monarchism
				traits = {
					elected_monarch 
				}
			}
        }			
	    ai_will_do = {
			factor = 1
		}
    }

		available = {
			has_government = monarchist
			monarchist > 0.4
			NOT = { has_global_flag = august_wilhelm_hohenzollern_flag }
		}
		
		fire_only_once = yes
		
		visible = { 
		    has_government = monarchist
            has_country_flag = electing_hohenzollerns			
			NOT = { has_country_flag = elected_king }
			NOT = { has_global_flag = august_wilhelm_hohenzollern_flag }
		}	
		
		complete_effect = {
		    clr_country_flag = electing_hohenzollerns
			set_country_flag = elected_king
			set_global_flag = august_wilhelm_hohenzollern_flag
			kill_country_leader = yes
			create_country_leader = {
					name = "August Wilhelm von Hohenzollern"
					picture = "gfx/leaders/Monarchs/Portrait_August_Wilhelm_Hohenzollern.tga"
					expire = "1981.1.1"
     				ideology = constitutional_monarchism
				traits = {
					elected_monarch anti_democrat
				}
			}
        }			
	    ai_will_do = {
			factor = 1
		}
    }

		    clr_country_flag = electing_bourbons
			set_country_flag = elected_king
			set_global_flag = jose_eugenio_baviera_flag

        }

		}
